   315 | >>> 
   316 | >>> ## About
   317 | >>> 
   318 | >>> Create your command-line parser, with all of the bells and whistles, declaratively or procedurally.
   319 | >>> 
   320 | >>> ### Example
   321 | >>> 
   322 | >>> This uses our
   323 | >>> [Derive API](https://docs.rs/clap/latest/clap/_derive/index.html)
   324 | >>> which provides access to the [Builder API](https://docs.rs/clap/latest/clap/index.html) as attributes on a `struct`:
   325 | >>> 
   326 | >>> <!-- Copied from examples/demo.{rs,md} -->
   327 | >>> ```rust
   328 | >>> use clap::Parser;
   329 | >>> 
   330 | >>> /// Simple program to greet a person
   331 | >>> #[derive(Parser, Debug)]
   332 | >>> #[command(version, about, long_about = None)]
   333 | >>> struct Args {
   334 | >>>     /// Name of the person to greet
   335 | >>>     #[arg(short, long)]
   336 | >>>     name: String,
   337 | >>> 
   338 | >>>     /// Number of times to greet
   339 | >>>     #[arg(short, long, default_value_t = 1)]
   340 | >>>     count: u8,
   341 | >>> }
   342 | >>> 
   343 | >>> fn main() {
   344 | >>>     let args = Args::parse();
   345 | >>> 
   346 | >>>     for _ in 0..args.count {
   347 | >>>         println!("Hello {}!", args.name);
   348 | >>>     }
   349 | >>> }
   350 | >>> ```
   351 | >>> 
   352 | >>> Add this to `Cargo.toml`:
   353 | >>> ```toml
   354 | >>> [dependencies]
   355 | >>> clap = { version = "4.5.45", features = ["derive"] }
   356 | >>> ```
   357 | >>> 
   358 | >>> You can then run your application with:
   359 | >>> ```console
   360 | >>> $ demo --help
   361 | >>> A simple to use, efficient, and full-featured Command Line Argument Parser
   362 | >>> 
   363 | >>> Usage: demo[EXE] [OPTIONS] --name <NAME>
   364 | >>> 
   365 | >>> Options:
   366 | >>>   -n, --name <NAME>    Name of the person to greet
   367 | >>>   -c, --count <COUNT>  Number of times to greet [default: 1]
   368 | >>>   -h, --help           Print help
   369 | >>>   -V, --version        Print version
   370 | >>> 
   371 | >>> $ demo --name Me
   372 | >>> Hello Me!
   373 | >>> ```
   374 | >>> 
   375 | >>> ### Aspirations
   376 | >>> 
   377 | >>> - Out of the box, users get a polished CLI experience
   378 | >>>   - Including common argument behavior, help generation, suggested fixes for users, colored output, [shell completions](https://github.com/clap-rs/clap

      && rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-src \
      && rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown wasm32-wasip2 \
      && rustup toolchain install nightly --component rustfmt clippy rust-src

      && cargo install cargo-tarpaulin \
      && cargo install cargo-release \
      && cargo install cargo-workspaces \
      && cargo install cargo-deny \

  ## About
  Create your command-line parser, with all of the bells and whistles, declaratively or procedurally.
  ### Example
  This uses our
  [Derive API](https://docs.rs/clap/latest/clap/_derive/index.html)
  which provides access to the [Builder API](https://docs.rs/clap/latest/clap/index.html) as attributes on a `struct`:
  <!-- Copied from examples/demo.{rs,md} -->
  ```rust
  use clap::Parser;
  /// Simple program to greet a person
  #[derive(Parser, Debug)]
  #[command(version, about, long_about = None)]
  struct Args {
      /// Name of the person to greet
      #[arg(short, long)]
      name: String,
      /// Number of times to greet
      #[arg(short, long, default_value_t = 1)]
      count: u8,
  }
  fn main() {
      let args = Args::parse();
      for _ in 0..args.count {
          println!("Hello {}!", args.name);
      }
  }
  ```
  Add this to `Cargo.toml`:
  ```toml
  [dependencies]
  clap = { version = "4.5.45", features = ["derive"] }
  ```
  You can then run your application with:
  ```console
  $ demo --help
  A simple to use, efficient, and full-featured Command Line Argument Parser
  Usage: demo[EXE] [OPTIONS] --name <NAME>
  Options:
    -n, --name <NAME>    Name of the person to greet
    -c, --count <COUNT>  Number of times to greet [default: 1]
    -h, --help           Print help
    -V, --version        Print version
  $ demo --name Me
  Hello Me!
  ```
  ### Aspirations
  - Out of the box, users get a polished CLI experience
    - Including common argument behavior, help generation, suggested fixes for users, colored output, [shell completions](https://github.com/clap-rs/clap

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.89.0
  ENV NODE_VERSION=20.x
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      make \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      fish \
      zsh \
      bash \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION} --profile minimal \
      && rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-src \
      && rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown wasm32-wasip2 \
      && rustup toolchain install nightly --component rustfmt clippy rust-src
  RUN cargo install cargo-edit \
      && cargo install cargo-tarpaulin \
      && cargo install cargo-release \
      && cargo install cargo-workspaces \
      && cargo install cargo-deny \
      && cargo install cargo-xtask \
      && cargo install typos-cli \
      && cargo install committed
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_${NODE_VERSION} | bash - \
      && apt-get install -y nodejs \
      && npm install -g renovate
  RUN pip3 install pre-commit
  RUN wget https://github.com/elves/elvish/releases/download/v0.20.1/elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
      && mv elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64/elvish /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64*
  RUN wget https://github.com/nushell/nushell/releases/download/0.99.1/nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && mv nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/nu /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN cargo build --all
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.89.0
  ENV NODE_VERSION=20.x
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      make \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      fish \
      zsh \
      bash \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION} --profile minimal \
      && . $CARGO_HOME/env \
      && rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-src \
      && rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown wasm32-wasip2 \
      && rustup toolchain install nightly --component rustfmt clippy rust-src
  RUN cargo install cargo-edit \
      && cargo install cargo-tarpaulin \
      && cargo install cargo-release \
      && cargo install cargo-workspaces \
      && cargo install cargo-deny \
      && cargo install cargo-xtask \
      && cargo install typos-cli \
      && cargo install committed
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_${NODE_VERSION} | bash - \
      && apt-get install -y nodejs \
      && npm install -g renovate
  RUN pip3 install pre-commit
  RUN wget https://github.com/elves/elvish/releases/download/v0.20.1/elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
      && mv elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64/elvish /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64*
  RUN wget https://github.com/nushell/nushell/releases/download/0.99.1/nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && mv nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/nu /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN cargo build --all
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  The Dockerfile has been created with most required tools and dependencies. The build is failing at line 32 when trying to install the nightly toolchain with components. The error occurs because the nightly toolchain installation is trying to add components that may already be installed or have conflicts with the stable toolchain components.
  next step
  Remove the `--component rustfmt clippy rust-src` flags from the nightly toolchain installation command on line 32, since these components are already installed for the stable toolchain on line 28. Change line 32 to:
  ```
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup toolchain install nightly
  ```

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.89.0
  ENV NODE_VERSION=20.x
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      make \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      fish \
      zsh \
      bash \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION} --profile minimal
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-src
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown wasm32-wasip2
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup toolchain install nightly --component rustfmt clippy rust-src
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo install cargo-edit \
      && cargo install cargo-tarpaulin \
      && cargo install cargo-release \
      && cargo install cargo-workspaces \
      && cargo install cargo-deny \
      && cargo install cargo-xtask \
      && cargo install typos-cli \
      && cargo install committed
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_${NODE_VERSION} | bash - \
      && apt-get install -y nodejs \
      && npm install -g renovate
  RUN pip3 install pre-commit
  RUN wget https://github.com/elves/elvish/releases/download/v0.20.1/elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64.tar.gz \
      && mv elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64/elvish /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64*
  RUN wget https://github.com/nushell/nushell/releases/download/0.99.1/nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && mv nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/nu /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo build --all
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      && mv elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64/elvish /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf elvish-v0.20.1-linux-amd64*
  RUN wget https://github.com/nushell/nushell/releases/download/0.99.1/nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && mv nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/nu /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo build --all
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.89.0
  ENV NODE_VERSION=20.x
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      make \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      fish \
      zsh \
      bash \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION} --profile minimal
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-src
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown wasm32-wasip2
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup toolchain install nightly
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo install cargo-edit \
      && cargo install cargo-tarpaulin \
      && cargo install cargo-release \
      && cargo install cargo-workspaces \
      && cargo install cargo-deny \
      && cargo install cargo-xtask \
      && cargo install typos-cli \
      && cargo install committed
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_${NODE_VERSION} | bash - \
      && apt-get install -y nodejs \
      && npm install -g renovate
  RUN pip3 install pre-commit
  RUN curl -L https://dl.elv.sh/linux-amd64/elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz -o elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz \
      && mv elvish-v0.20.1/elvish /usr/local/bin/ \
      && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/elvish \
      && rm -rf elvish-v0.20.1*
  RUN wget https://github.com/nushell/nushell/releases/download/0.99.1/nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && mv nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/nu /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo build --all
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.89.0
  ENV NODE_VERSION=20.x
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      make \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      fish \
      zsh \
      bash \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION} --profile minimal
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-src
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown wasm32-wasip2
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup toolchain install nightly
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo install cargo-edit \
      && cargo install cargo-tarpaulin \
      && cargo install cargo-release \
      && cargo install cargo-workspaces \
      && cargo install cargo-deny \
      && cargo install cargo-xtask \
      && cargo install typos-cli \
      && cargo install committed
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_${NODE_VERSION} | bash - \
      && apt-get install -y nodejs \
      && npm install -g renovate
  RUN pip3 install pre-commit
  RUN curl -L https://dl.elv.sh/linux-amd64/elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz -o elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz \
      && mv elvish /usr/local/bin/ \
      && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/elvish \
      && rm -rf elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz
  RUN wget https://github.com/nushell/nushell/releases/download/0.99.1/nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && mv nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/nu /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo build --all
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.89.0
  ENV NODE_VERSION=20.x
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      make \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      fish \
      zsh \
      bash \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION} --profile minimal
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-src
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown wasm32-wasip2
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup toolchain install nightly
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo install cargo-edit \
      && cargo install cargo-tarpaulin \
      && cargo install cargo-release \
      && cargo install cargo-workspaces \
      && cargo install cargo-deny \
      && cargo install cargo-xtask \
      && cargo install typos-cli \
      && cargo install committed
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_${NODE_VERSION} | bash - \
      && apt-get install -y nodejs \
      && npm install -g renovate
  RUN pip3 install pre-commit
  RUN curl -L https://dl.elv.sh/linux-amd64/elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz -o elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz \
      && mv elvish-v0.20.1/elvish /usr/local/bin/ \
      && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/elvish \
      && rm -rf elvish-v0.20.1*
  RUN wget https://github.com/nushell/nushell/releases/download/0.99.1/nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && mv nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/nu /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo build --all
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.89.0
  ENV NODE_VERSION=20.x
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      make \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      fish \
      zsh \
      bash \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION} --profile minimal
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-src
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown wasm32-wasip2
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup toolchain install nightly
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo install cargo-edit \
      && cargo install cargo-tarpaulin \
      && cargo install cargo-release \
      && cargo install cargo-workspaces \
      && cargo install cargo-deny \
      && cargo install cargo-xtask \
      && cargo install typos-cli \
      && cargo install committed
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_${NODE_VERSION} | bash - \
      && apt-get install -y nodejs \
      && npm install -g renovate
  RUN pip3 install pre-commit
  RUN curl -L https://dl.elv.sh/linux-amd64/elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz -o elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz \
      && mv elvish /usr/local/bin/ \
      && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/elvish \
      && rm -rf elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz
  RUN wget https://github.com/nushell/nushell/releases/download/0.99.1/nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && mv nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/nu /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo build --all
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.89.0
  ENV NODE_VERSION=20.x
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup
  ENV PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      make \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      fish \
      zsh \
      bash \
      wget \
      ca-certificates \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION} --profile minimal
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-src
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown wasm32-wasip2
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && rustup toolchain install nightly
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo install cargo-edit \
      && cargo install cargo-tarpaulin \
      && cargo install cargo-release \
      && cargo install cargo-workspaces \
      && cargo install cargo-deny \
      && cargo install cargo-xtask \
      && cargo install typos-cli \
      && cargo install committed
  RUN curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_${NODE_VERSION} | bash - \
      && apt-get install -y nodejs \
      && npm install -g renovate
  RUN pip3 install pre-commit
  RUN curl -L https://dl.elv.sh/linux-amd64/elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz -o elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz \
      && mkdir -p /tmp/elvish-extract \
      && tar -xzf elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz -C /tmp/elvish-extract \
      && find /tmp/elvish-extract -name "elvish*" -type f -executable -exec mv {} /usr/local/bin/elvish \; \
      && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/elvish \
      && rm -rf elvish-v0.20.1.tar.gz /tmp/elvish-extract
  RUN wget https://github.com/nushell/nushell/releases/download/0.99.1/nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && tar -xzf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu.tar.gz \
      && mv nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu/nu /usr/local/bin/ \
      && rm -rf nu-0.99.1-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && cargo build --all
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
